| <span data-ttu-id="60cae-842">Entrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="60cae-842">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="60cae-843">Value</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="60cae-843">Value</span></span> |
